			<article id="post-9949" class="post-9949 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-blog category-judiciary category-newsupdates tag-class-8-social-science-book tag-corruption-in-judiciary-textbook tag-exploring-society-india-and-beyond tag-judiciary-chapter-controversy tag-judiciary-institutional-integrity tag-ncert-director-notice tag-ncert-textbook-ban tag-school-curriculum-controversy-india tag-supreme-court-blanket-ban tag-supreme-court-of-india infinite-scroll-item no-featured-image-padding" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork" itemscope>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/supreme-court-of-india-orders-blanket-ban-on-ncert-class-8-social-science-textbook/" rel="bookmark">Supreme Court of India Orders Blanket Ban on NCERT Class 8 Social Science Textbook</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-26T21:49:22+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">26 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>
					</header>
			<div class="post-image">
						
						<a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/supreme-court-of-india-orders-blanket-ban-on-ncert-class-8-social-science-textbook/">
							<img width="768" height="512" src="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-26-2026-09_43_46-PM-768x512.png" class="attachment-medium_large size-medium_large wp-post-image" alt="" itemprop="image" decoding="async" fetchpriority="high" srcset="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-26-2026-09_43_46-PM-768x512.png 768w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-26-2026-09_43_46-PM-300x200.png 300w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-26-2026-09_43_46-PM-1024x683.png 1024w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-26-2026-09_43_46-PM.png 1536w" sizes="(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" />

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant development on February 26, 2026, the Supreme Court of India ordered a blanket ban on a Class 8 Social Science textbook published by National Council of Educational Research and Training (NCERT). The book, titled Exploring Society: India and Beyond, has &#8230; </p>
<p class="read-more-container"><a title="Supreme Court of India Orders Blanket Ban on NCERT Class 8 Social Science Textbook" class="read-more button" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/supreme-court-of-india-orders-blanket-ban-on-ncert-class-8-social-science-textbook/#more-9949" aria-label="Read more about Supreme Court of India Orders Blanket Ban on NCERT Class 8 Social Science Textbook">Read more</a></p>

				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/punjab-and-haryana-high-court-clarifies-harmless-compliment-does-not-automatically-amount-to-sexual-harassment/" rel="bookmark">Punjab and Haryana High Court Clarifies: Harmless Compliment Does Not Automatically Amount to Sexual Harassment</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-26T21:22:22+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">26 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling dated February 26, 2026, the Punjab and Haryana High Court addressed an important question: Can a poetic compliment posted in a WhatsApp group amount to sexual harassment? The case involved a man who commented on a woman’s photograph &#8230; </p>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling impacting distance technical education in India, the Supreme Court has reaffirmed the authority of the University Grants Commission (UGC) to take action on questionable technical degrees awarded through distance learning mode. The decision came in University Grants Commission vs. &#8230; </p>

			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-26T17:00:13+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">26 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling, the Madras High Court has reaffirmed that procedural technicalities should not defeat substantive justice under the GST regime. The Court condoned a delay in filing an appeal where the assessee was bona fide pursuing a rectification application before &#8230; </p>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/madras-high-court-hospitals-cannot-enforce-non-compete-clauses-against-doctors/" rel="bookmark">Madras High Court: Hospitals Cannot Enforce Non-Compete Clauses Against Doctors</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-25T22:32:18+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">25 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>
					</header>
			<div class="post-image">
						
						<a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/madras-high-court-hospitals-cannot-enforce-non-compete-clauses-against-doctors/">
							<img width="768" height="454" src="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260225_222314-1-768x454.png" class="attachment-medium_large size-medium_large wp-post-image" alt="" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260225_222314-1-768x454.png 768w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260225_222314-1-300x177.png 300w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260225_222314-1-1024x605.png 1024w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260225_222314-1.png 1536w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" />

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a landmark ruling, the Madras High Court has held that private hospitals cannot treat doctors like factory workmen by imposing restrictive non-compete and non-solicitation clauses in professional agreements. The Court emphasized that hospitals are service-oriented institutions and cannot function as profit-driven &#8230; </p>
<p class="read-more-container"><a title="Madras High Court: Hospitals Cannot Enforce Non-Compete Clauses Against Doctors" class="read-more button" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/madras-high-court-hospitals-cannot-enforce-non-compete-clauses-against-doctors/#more-9928" aria-label="Read more about Madras High Court: Hospitals Cannot Enforce Non-Compete Clauses Against Doctors">Read more</a></p>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/supreme-court-reaffirms-bail-cannot-be-cancelled-merely-due-to-addition-of-new-offences/" rel="bookmark">Supreme Court Reaffirms: Bail Cannot Be Cancelled Merely Due to Addition of New Offences</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-25T16:53:37+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">25 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In Sumit v. State of U.P. and Another, the Supreme Court of India delivered a significant judgment in February 2026 reaffirming the constitutional sanctity of personal liberty in bail jurisprudence. The Court held that once bail has been granted by a competent court, &#8230; </p>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/delhi-high-court-sets-aside-rejection-of-gst-registration-restoration/" rel="bookmark">Delhi High Court Sets Aside Rejection of GST Registration Restoration</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-25T12:54:33+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">25 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>
					</header>
			<div class="post-image">

							<img width="768" height="463" src="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot_2026-02-25-12-49-39-32_680d03679600f7af0b4c700c6b270fe7-768x463.jpg" class="attachment-medium_large size-medium_large wp-post-image" alt="" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot_2026-02-25-12-49-39-32_680d03679600f7af0b4c700c6b270fe7-768x463.jpg 768w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot_2026-02-25-12-49-39-32_680d03679600f7af0b4c700c6b270fe7-300x181.jpg 300w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot_2026-02-25-12-49-39-32_680d03679600f7af0b4c700c6b270fe7-1024x617.jpg 1024w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot_2026-02-25-12-49-39-32_680d03679600f7af0b4c700c6b270fe7.jpg 1079w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" />
						</a>
					</div>
			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling strengthening procedural fairness under GST law, the Delhi High Court set aside the rejection of a taxpayer’s application for restoration of GST registration in Param Infrawell Private Limited v. State of NCT of Delhi &amp; Others ([2026] 183 taxmann.com 557). &#8230; </p>
<p class="read-more-container"><a title="Delhi High Court Sets Aside Rejection of GST Registration Restoration" class="read-more button" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/delhi-high-court-sets-aside-rejection-of-gst-registration-restoration/#more-9921" aria-label="Read more about Delhi High Court Sets Aside Rejection of GST Registration Restoration">Read more</a></p>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/delhi-high-court-rejects-the-idle-wife-myth-homemakers-labour-recognised-as-real-economic-contribution/" rel="bookmark">Delhi High Court Rejects the “Idle Wife” Myth: Homemaker’s Labour Recognised as Real Economic Contribution</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-24T22:35:09+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">24 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="post-image">

							<img width="768" height="444" src="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260224_223152-768x444.png" class="attachment-medium_large size-medium_large wp-post-image" alt="" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260224_223152-768x444.png 768w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260224_223152-300x173.png 300w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/IMG_20260224_223152.png 1024w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" />

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling delivered in February 2026, the Delhi High Court firmly rejected the outdated notion of the “idle wife,” holding that a homemaker’s unpaid domestic labour must be recognised as a substantial economic contribution while determining maintenance. Justice &#8230; </p>

				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/kerala-high-court-criminal-proceedings-in-rape-pocso-cases-can-be-quashed-in-exceptional-circumstances/" rel="bookmark">Kerala High Court: Criminal Proceedings in Rape &#038; POCSO Cases Can Be Quashed in “Exceptional Circumstances”</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant development, the Kerala High Court has reiterated that criminal proceedings in rape and Protection of Children from Sexual Offences (POCSO) cases may be quashed in exceptional circumstances—particularly where the accused and the victim have subsequently married and are &#8230; </p>

				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/provisional-attachment-under-gst-cannot-continue-beyond-one-year-calcutta-high-court-clarifies-section-832/" rel="bookmark">Provisional Attachment Under GST Cannot Continue Beyond One Year: Calcutta High Court Clarifies Section 83(2)</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-24T10:05:44+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">24 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling, the Calcutta High Court has reaffirmed that provisional attachment of bank accounts under Section 83 of the Central Goods and Services Tax Act, 2017 (CGST Act) automatically lapses after one year. The Court held that such &#8230; </p>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/telangana-high-court-condoned-202-day-delay-in-itat-appeal-due-to-covid-19-business-disruption/" rel="bookmark">Telangana High Court Condoned 202-Day Delay in ITAT Appeal Due to COVID-19 Business Disruption</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-23T18:27:27+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">23 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling reinforcing a justice-oriented approach, the Telangana High Court condoned a delay of 202 days in filing an appeal before the Income Tax Appellate Tribunal (ITAT), acknowledging the severe impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on business operations. The decision, &#8230; </p>

				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/supreme-court-examines-constitutional-validity-of-income-tax-search-powers-over-digital-data/" rel="bookmark">Supreme Court Examines Constitutional Validity of Income Tax Search Powers Over Digital Data</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-23T16:46:07+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">23 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>The Supreme Court of India is currently hearing a significant public interest litigation (PIL) that questions the constitutional validity of the Income Tax Department’s powers to conduct search and seizure operations—particularly involving digital devices—without prior notice. The petition has been &#8230; </p>

	<div class="inside-article">
					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/kerala-high-court-employer-cannot-force-employee-to-continue-in-service-after-valid-resignation/" rel="bookmark">Kerala High Court: Employer Cannot Force Employee to Continue in Service After Valid Resignation</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-22T20:11:21+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">22 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>
					</header>
			<div class="post-image">
						
						<a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/kerala-high-court-employer-cannot-force-employee-to-continue-in-service-after-valid-resignation/">
							<img width="768" height="512" src="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-22-2026-08_04_07-PM-768x512.png" class="attachment-medium_large size-medium_large wp-post-image" alt="" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-22-2026-08_04_07-PM-768x512.png 768w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-22-2026-08_04_07-PM-300x200.png 300w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-22-2026-08_04_07-PM-1024x683.png 1024w, https://anptaxcorp.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ChatGPT-Image-Feb-22-2026-08_04_07-PM.png 1536w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" />

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant February 2026 judgment, the Kerala High Court reaffirmed a fundamental principle of employment law — no employer can compel an employee to remain in service once a valid resignation has been submitted in accordance with contractual terms. &#8230; </p>
<p class="read-more-container"><a title="Kerala High Court: Employer Cannot Force Employee to Continue in Service After Valid Resignation" class="read-more button" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/kerala-high-court-employer-cannot-force-employee-to-continue-in-service-after-valid-resignation/#more-9899" aria-label="Read more about Kerala High Court: Employer Cannot Force Employee to Continue in Service After Valid Resignation">Read more</a></p>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a thought-provoking keynote address on 14 February 2026, CJI Surya Kant called for a fundamental rethinking of how judicial leadership is perceived and practiced. Speaking at the 11th Commonwealth Judicial Educators’ Conference in New Delhi, the Chief Justice emphasized that the strength of &#8230; </p>

					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/single-slap-not-cruelty-under-section-498a-gujarat-high-court-acquits-husband-after-23-years/" rel="bookmark">‘Single Slap’ Not Cruelty Under Section 498A: Gujarat High Court Acquits Husband After 23 Years</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-22T17:18:52+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">22 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling, the Gujarat High Court has held that a single instance of a husband slapping his wife, without proof of sustained harassment, does not amount to “cruelty” under Section 498A of the Indian Penal Code (IPC). The Court set &#8230; </p>

	<div class="inside-article">
					<header class="entry-header">
				<h2 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://anptaxcorp.com/delhi-high-court-wife-may-have-to-repay-interim-maintenance-with-6-interest-if-adultery-is-proven/" rel="bookmark">Delhi High Court: Wife May Have to Repay Interim Maintenance with 6% Interest if Adultery is Proven</a></h2>		<div class="entry-meta">
			<span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-22T14:31:51+05:30" itemprop="datePublished">22 February 2026</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://anptaxcorp.com/author/aditya/" title="View all posts by Aditya Narayan Parida" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">Aditya Narayan Parida</span></a></span></span> 		</div>

			<div class="post-image">

			<div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text">
				<p>In a significant ruling delivered in February 2026, the Delhi High Court held that a wife may be required to refund the entire amount of interim maintenance received—along with 6% interest—if allegations of adultery against her are ultimately proved during trial. The &#8230; </p>
